msg:The hotel staff were friendly and helpful.  I arrived in the early evening and was quickly checked in.  They were clear with directions to my hotel room, where breakfast was served, and where the pool and gym were.  The day before I checked out, I needed to get a Covid test done and they directed me to the hospital doing these tests.  Even on the day of check out, my flight wasn‚Äôt until 7pm so they held onto my bags for me while I enjoy almost a whole full day on the beach.

The hotel‚Äôs location is great too.  It‚Äôs about a casual 15 minute stroll to Dadonghai and the restaurants in that area.  It‚Äôs also about a 10 minute walk from the popular night market.

Back inside the hotel, the rooms are comfortable and have great views.  The only issue I had was the lack of equipment in the gym.  While it did have everything one might need for a workout I felt it was missing one or two pieces of equipment that would make a workout feel complete.  The pool is right outside the gym and is great!  Comfortable location that gets sun for most of the morning but by 1 or 2 starts to become shaded by the building.  My only issue with the pool is that it was too cold.  The temperature they had written on the whiteboard nearby said it was 24c but, it felt much colder than that.

All together, I would highly recommend this hotel to anyone coming to visit Sanya.

msg:Crowne Plaza Sanya City Centre is a hotel from IHG group. It has everything what a traveller would need. The building and room facilities are in excellent conditions even the property has several years. My room was located in the 20th floor and even had some construction going on, no noise disturbing issues I had during my stay. The view over the city was phenomenal and very quite to seat at the balcony and get some food or a drink.

Every staff that I encountered proactively offer greeting which is not very common to see in hotels in China.

Furthermore, I would like to express my gratitude to Mrs. Eason Feng at the Front Desk who assisted me with my Check-In process very efficiently and without any inconvenient. As well, Mrs. Lavender at the fitness center who went beyond his work to assist me with some take-away issues and room service information (I can not read Chinese); In addition provided me excellent service at the gym and pool.
Last, but no least I would like thank Mr. Jodie Chen at the front desk who help me with my check out process in an excellent manner, following all IHG standards and  being flexible to my request. I thank him
 a lot.

The property is located right in city centre and very convenient to explore the city of Sanya. For the price it's an excellent choice in the city and totally recommend everyone to book this hotel.
